     -- Topology identifiability N_down vs N_up         --
     --------------------------------------------------------
     -- To run in console: cat ndown-nup.m2 | M2 &> ndown-nup_out.txt
     -- we call z's the variables on N_down, and w's the variables in N_up
     -- gz: gamma for N_down; gw: gamma for N_up
